  <COMMENT line1="11" col1="1" line2="11" col2="78" start="1200" end="1277">#' sample. Putting more than one sample's results in the directory will result</COMMENT>

  <COMMENT line1="13" col1="1" line2="13" col2="62" start="1418" end="1479">#' files (with the default names given by Salmon) 'quant.sf', </COMMENT>

  <COMMENT line1="19" col1="1" line2="19" col2="79" start="2072" end="2150">#' This function will work for Salmon v0.7.x and greater, as the name of one of</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="20" col1="1" line2="20" col2="74" start="2181" end="2254">#' the default output directories was changed from "aux" to "aux_info" in </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="21" col1="1" line2="21" col2="15" start="2290" end="2304">#' Salmon v0.7.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="22" col1="1" line2="22" col2="3" start="2399" end="2401">#' </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="23" col1="1" line2="23" col2="76" start="2508" end="2583">#' @return A list with two elements: (1) a data.frame \code{abundance} with </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="24" col1="1" line2="24" col2="78" start="2617" end="2694">#' columns for 'target_id' (feature, transcript, gene etc), 'length' (feature </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="25" col1="1" line2="25" col2="76" start="2726" end="2801">#' length), 'est_counts' (estimated feature counts), 'tpm' (transcripts per </COMMENT>

  <COMMENT line1="27" col1="1" line2="27" col2="71" start="2944" end="3014">#' generated the results, including number of reads processed, mapping </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="28" col1="1" line2="28" col2="85" start="3053" end="3137">#' percentage, the library type used for the RNA-sequencing, including details about </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="29" col1="1" line2="29" col2="73" start="3162" end="3234">#' number of reads that did not match the given or inferred library type,</COMMENT>

  <COMMENT line1="256" col1="1" line2="256" col2="58" start="27905" end="27962">#' Run Salmon on FASTQ files to quantify feature abundance</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="257" col1="1" line2="257" col2="2" start="28014" end="28015">#'</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="258" col1="1" line2="258" col2="72" start="28123" end="28194">#' Run the abundance quantification tool \code{Salmon} on a set of FASTQ</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="259" col1="1" line2="259" col2="78" start="28232" end="28309">#' files. Requires \code{Salmon} (\url{https://combine-lab.github.io/salmon/})</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="260" col1="1" line2="260" col2="79" start="28341" end="28419">#' to be installed and a Salmon transcript index must have been generated prior</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="261" col1="1" line2="261" col2="76" start="28450" end="28525">#' to using this function. See the Salmon website for installation and basic</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="262" col1="1" line2="262" col2="22" start="28559" end="28580">#' usage instructions.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="263" col1="1" line2="263" col2="2" start="28668" end="28669">#'</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="264" col1="1" line2="264" col2="79" start="28777" end="28855">#' @param targets_file character string giving the path to a tab-delimited text</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="265" col1="1" line2="265" col2="80" start="28886" end="28965">#' file with either 2 columns (single-end reads) or 3 columns (paired-end reads)</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="266" col1="1" line2="266" col2="80" start="28995" end="29074">#' that gives the sample names (first column) and FastQ file names (column 2 and</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="267" col1="1" line2="267" col2="79" start="29104" end="29182">#' if applicable 3). The file is assumed to have column headers, although these</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="268" col1="1" line2="268" col2="16" start="29213" end="29228">#' are not used.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="269" col1="1" line2="269" col2="73" start="29322" end="29394">#' @param transcript_index character string giving the path to the Salmon</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="270" col1="1" line2="270" col2="61" start="29431" end="29491">#' index to be used for the feature abundance quantification.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="271" col1="1" line2="271" col2="77" start="29540" end="29616">#' @param single_end logical, are single-end reads used, or paired-end reads?</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="272" col1="1" line2="272" col2="80" start="29649" end="29728">#' @param output_prefix character string giving the prefix for the output folder</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="273" col1="1" line2="273" col2="75" start="29758" end="29832">#' that will contain the Salmon results. The default is \code{"output"} and</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="274" col1="1" line2="274" col2="80" start="29867" end="29946">#' the sample name (column 1 of \code{targets_file}) is appended (preceded by an</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="275" col1="1" line2="275" col2="15" start="29976" end="29990">#' underscore).</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="276" col1="1" line2="276" col2="71" start="30085" end="30155">#' @param lib_type scalar, indicating RNA-seq library type. See Salmon </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="277" col1="1" line2="277" col2="70" start="30194" end="30263">#' documentation for details. Default is "A", for automatic detection.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="278" col1="1" line2="278" col2="71" start="30303" end="30373">#' @param n_processes integer giving the number of processes to use for</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="279" col1="1" line2="279" col2="77" start="30412" end="30488">#' parallel Salmon jobs across samples. The package \code{parallel} is used. </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="280" col1="1" line2="280" col2="37" start="30521" end="30557">#' Default is 2 concurrent processes.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="281" col1="1" line2="281" col2="78" start="30630" end="30707">#' @param n_thread_per_process integer giving the number of threads for Salmon</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="282" col1="1" line2="282" col2="79" start="30739" end="30817">#' to use per process (to parallelize Salmon for a given sample). Default is 4.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="283" col1="1" line2="283" col2="76" start="30848" end="30923">#' @param n_bootstrap_samples integer giving the number of bootstrap samples</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="284" col1="1" line2="284" col2="77" start="30957" end="31033">#' that Salmon should use (default is 0). With bootstrap samples, uncertainty</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="285" col1="1" line2="285" col2="34" start="31066" end="31099">#' in abundance can be quantified.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="286" col1="1" line2="286" col2="78" start="31175" end="31252">#' @param seqBias logical, should Salmon's option be used to model and correct</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="287" col1="1" line2="287" col2="65" start="31284" end="31348">#' abundances for sequence specific bias? Default is \code{TRUE}.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="288" col1="1" line2="288" col2="77" start="31393" end="31469">#' @param gcBias logical, should Salmon's option be used to model and correct</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="289" col1="1" line2="289" col2="76" start="31502" end="31577">#' abundances for GC content bias? Requires Salmon version 0.7.2 or higher. </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="290" col1="1" line2="290" col2="26" start="31611" end="31636">#' Default is \code{TRUE}.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="291" col1="1" line2="291" col2="78" start="31720" end="31797">#' @param posBias logical, should Salmon's option be used to model and correct</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="292" col1="1" line2="292" col2="77" start="31829" end="31905">#' abundances for positional biases? Requires Salmon version 0.7.3 or higher.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="293" col1="1" line2="293" col2="27" start="31938" end="31964">#' Default is \code{FALSE}.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="294" col1="1" line2="294" col2="75" start="32047" end="32121">#' @param allowOrphans logical, Consider orphaned reads as valid hits when </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="295" col1="1" line2="295" col2="75" start="32156" end="32230">#' performing lightweight-alignment. This option will increase sensitivity </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="296" col1="1" line2="296" col2="74" start="32265" end="32338">#' (allow more reads to map and more transcripts to be detected), but may </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="297" col1="1" line2="297" col2="78" start="32374" end="32451">#' decrease specificity as orphaned alignments are more likely to be spurious.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="298" col1="1" line2="298" col2="45" start="32483" end="32527">#' For more details see Salmon documentation.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="299" col1="1" line2="299" col2="75" start="32592" end="32666">#' @param advanced_opts character scalar supplying list of advanced option </COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="300" col1="1" line2="300" col2="79" start="32701" end="32779">#' arguments to apply to each Salmon call. For details see Salmon documentation</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="301" col1="1" line2="301" col2="64" start="32810" end="32873">#' or type \code{salmon quant --help-reads} at the command line.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="302" col1="1" line2="302" col2="75" start="32919" end="32993">#' @param dry_run logical, if \code{TRUE} then a list containing the Salmon</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="303" col1="1" line2="303" col2="76" start="33028" end="33103">#' commands that would be run and the output directories is returned. Can be</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="304" col1="1" line2="304" col2="78" start="33137" end="33214">#' used to read in results if Salmon is run outside an R session or to produce</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="305" col1="1" line2="305" col2="44" start="33246" end="33289">#'  a script to run outside of an R session.</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="306" col1="1" line2="306" col2="73" start="33355" end="33427">#' @param salmon_cmd (optional) string giving full command to use to call</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="307" col1="1" line2="307" col2="74" start="33464" end="33537">#' Salmon, if simply typing "salmon" at the command line does not give the</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="308" col1="1" line2="308" col2="75" start="33573" end="33647">#' required version of Salmon or does not work. Default is simply "salmon".</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="309" col1="1" line2="309" col2="73" start="33682" end="33754">#' If used, this argument should give the full path to the desired Salmon</COMMENT>
  <COMMENT line1="310" col1="1" line2="310" col2="10" start="33791" end="33800">#' binary.</COMMENT>
